)@@G@@*****************************************LVALUE**JC00             @I@@@@OQ
)@@G@@. LVALUE  D1,D2.              'GET LEAST LENGTH VALUE'             JC00 OR
)@@G@@            @I@@@@.                                                     OS
)@@G@@             JC00             @I@@@@. CALCULATES THE MINIMUM SIZE OF THEOT
)@@G@@ PATTERN D2, AND PUTS IT INTO  JC00             @I@@@@. A(D1).  FV(D1) IOU
)@@G@@S SET TO 0.  A(D2) IS THE ADDRESS OF THE FIRST   JC00             @I@@@@OV
)@@G@@. NODE IN THE PATTERN, AND ALL POINTERS WITHIN THE PATTERN ARE     JC00 OW
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. RELATIVE TO THIS ADDRESS.  THE RELEVANT FIELDS WITHIOX
)@@G@@N A PATTERN  JC00             @I@@@@. NOTE, P, ARE:                     OY
)@@G@@                               JC00             @I@@@@.    A(P+2D) = ADDOZ
)@@G@@RESS (REL. TO A(D2)) OF THE NEXT NODE.           JC00             @I@@@@PA
)@@G@@.    A(P+3D) = SIZE OF NODE (MIN SIZE IT CAN MATCH).               JC00 PB
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. OF COURSE, A LINK OF 0 IS END-OF-PATTERN.  REWRITINGPC
)@@G@@ THIS        JC00             @I@@@@. PROC AS A SUBROUTINE CALL PROBABLYPD
)@@G@@ ISN'T WORTH THE EFFORT, SINCE JC00             @I@@@@. IT IS ONLY CALLEPE
)@@G@@D 6 TIMES.                                       JC00             @I@@@@PF
)@@G@@. LVALUE SHOULD WORK FOR A(D2) > 64K.                              JC00 PG
)@@G@@            @I@@@@.                                                     PH
)@@G@@             JC00             @I@@@@LVALUE**  PROC      1,10.           PI
)@@G@@                               JC00             @I@@@@          LA      PJ
)@@G@@  A0,LVALUE(1,2).     A(D2) = BASE ADDR OF PATTERJC00             @I@@@@PK
)@@G@@          LA        A1,6,A0.       INITIAL VALUE--SIZE OF 1ST NODE JC00 PL
)@@G@@            @I@@@@LOOP      TG        A1,6,A0.       TEST AGAINST MINIMUPM
)@@G@@M.           JC00             @I@@@@          LA        A1,6,A0.       IPN
)@@G@@F LESS, GRAB IT.               JC00             @I@@@@          LA      PO
)@@G@@  A0,4,A0.       GET REL ADDR OF NEXT NODE.      JC00             @I@@@@PP
)@@G@@          JZ        A0,$+3.        IF ZERO, END OF PATTERN         JC00 PQ
)@@G@@            @I@@@@          AA        A0,LVALUE(1,2).     ADD BASE TO NOPR
)@@G@@DE ADDR.     JC00             @I@@@@          J         LOOP.          PPS
)@@G@@ROCESS NEXT NODE.              JC00             @I@@@@DONE      SA      PT
)@@G@@  A1,LVALUE(1,1).     A(D1) GETS RESULT.         JC00             @I@@@@PU
)@@G@@          SZ        LVALUE(1,1)+1. F,V-FIELDS SET TO ZERO.         JC00 PV
)@@G@@            @I@]@@          LOFF.                                       PW
)@@G@@             JC00             @I[@@@          END.                      PX
)@@G@@                               JC00             @I@@@@. ****************PY

)@@G@@***********************MSLIM***JC09             @I@@@@. MSLIM  DE.      TU
)@@G@@            'GET TIME LIMIT IN MILLISECONDS'     JC09             @I@@@@TV
)@@G@@.                                                                  JC09 TW
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. THIS ASSIGNS TO A(DE) THE TIME LIMIT AS IT APPEARS OTX
)@@G@@N THE @RUN CAJC09             @I@@@@. IN MILLISECONDS.  AFTER THIS MUCH TY
)@@G@@TIME THE EXECUTIVE WILL TERMINAJC09             @I@@@@. THE JOB, SO IT BTZ
)@@G@@EHOOVES THE SNOBOL SYSTEM TO GET THERE FIRST IF IJC09             @I@@@@UA
)@@G@@. WANTS TO PRINT OUT ANY MESSAGES OF ITS OWN.  IT IS IN FACT USED  JC09 UB
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. TO SET UP A SNOBOL4 INTERRUPT JUST BEFORE THE SYSTEMUC
)@@G@@ ACTS, SO THEJC09             @I@@@@. USER WILL KNOW WHERE HE WAS KILLEDUD
)@@G@@, AND PERHAPS EVEN GIVE PART OFJC09             @I@@@@. DUMP IF REQUESTEUE
)@@G@@D.  IF NOT IMPLEMENTED ON A PARTICULAR SYSTEM,   JC09             @I@@@@UF
)@@G@@. THIS MACRO SHOULD RETURN THE LARGEST INTEGER POSSIBLE.  IF IT IS JC09 UG
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. IMPLEMENTED, THE VALUES ASSIGNED TO DE SHOULD BE:   UH
)@@G@@             JC09             @I@@@@.         A(DE) = TIME LIMIT IN MS. UI
)@@G@@(AS AN INTEGER)                JC09             @I@@@@.         F(DE) = UJ
)@@G@@0                                                JC09             @I@@@@UK
)@@G@@.         V(DE) = INTEGER DATA TYPE                                JC09 UL
)@@G@@            @I@@@@.                                                     UM
)@@G@@             JC09             @I@@@@. A0-A1 USED.                       UN
)@@G@@                               JC09             @I@@@@.                 UO
)@@G@@                                                 JC09             @I@@@@UP
)@@G@@MSLIM**   PROC      1.                                             JC09 UQ
)@@G@@            @I@@@@          LA        A0,(4,PCTBUF).                    UR
)@@G@@             JC09             @I@@@@          ER        PCT$.          GUS
)@@G@@ET PCT                         JC09             @I@@@@          LA      UT
)@@G@@  A0,PCTBUF+3.   3RD WORD = LIMIT, UNIT = .2 MS. JC09             @I@@@@UU
)@@G@@          DSL       A0,36.         CHANGE TO MS.                   JC09 UV
)@@G@@            @I@@@@          DI,U      A0,5.                             UW
)@@G@@             JC09             @I@@@@          SA        A0,MSLIM(1,1). PUX
)@@G@@UT IN A(DE)                    JC09             @I@@@@          LA,U    UY
)@@G@@  A0,INTDT.                                      JC09             @I@@@@UZ
)@@G@@          SA        A0,MSLIM(1,1)+1.    MARK AS INTEGER            JC09 VA
)@@G@@            @I@]@@          LOFF.                                       VB
)@@G@@             JC09             @I[@@@          END.                      VC
)@@G@@                               JC09             @I@@@@. ****************VD
)@@G@@*****************************************MSLIM***JC09             @I@@@@VE

)@@G@@*****************************************MULT****JC00             @I@[@@VT
)@@G@@MULT**    PROC      1.                 MULTIPLY INTEGERS                VU
)@@G@@            @I@[@@SAME      EQU       MULT(1,*4)**MULT(1,*5).           VV
)@@G@@                              @I@[@@  DO SAME , DL      A1,MULT(1,2).   VW
)@@G@@                                                @I@[@@  DO SAME , MSI   VX
)@@G@@  A1,MULT(1,3).                                                   @I@[@@VY
)@@G@@  DO 1-SAME , LA    A0,MULT(1,2).                                       VZ
)@@G@@            @I@[@@  DO 1-SAME , MF    A0,MULT(1,3).                     WA
)@@G@@                              @I@[@@  DO 1-SAME , JNZ   A0,GOOD.        WB
)@@G@@                                                @I@[@@  DO 1-SAME , DSA WC
)@@G@@  A0,1.                                                           @I@[@@WD
)@@G@@  DO 1-SAME , LA    A2,MULT(1,2)+1.                                     WE
)@@G@@            @I@[@@          DS        A1,MULT(1,1).                     WF
)@@G@@                              @I@[@@  DO 1-MULT(1,*5) , J MULT(1,5).    WG
)@@G@@                                                @I@[@@GOOD      LOCC    WH
)@@G@@  MULT(1,4),$.                                   JC02             @I@[@@WI
)@@G@@          END.                                                          WJ
)@@G@@            @G@@@[. MULT  D1,D2,D3,FAIL,SUCC.        'MULTIPLY INTEGERS'WK
)@@G@@             JC12 @G@@@[.                                               WL
)@@G@@                   JC12 @G@@@[. A(D1) := A(D2) * A(D3); FV(D1) := FV(D2)WM
)@@G@@                         JC12 @G@@@[.                                   WN
)@@G@@                               JC12 @G@@@[. A0-A2 USED.                 WO
)@@G@@                                     JC12 @G@@@[.                       WP
)@@G@@                                           JC12 @G@@@[MULT**    PROC    WQ
)@@G@@  1.                                             JC12 @G@@@[SE        EQWR
)@@G@@U       1-MULT(1,*5).  SUCCESS EXIT EXISTS.            JC12 @G@@@[.     WS
)@@G@@                                                             JC12 @G@@@[WT
)@@G@@          LA        A0,MULT(1,2).  A(D2).                          JC12 WU
)@@G@@@G@@@[          MI        A0,MULT(1,3).  * A(D2), TO A0/A1.             WV
)@@G@@ JC12 @G@@@[          JNZ       A0,FAIL.       FAIL IF RESULT TOO BIG.  WW
)@@G@@       JC12 @G@@@[          LA        A2,MULT(1,2)+1.  FV(D2).          WX
)@@G@@             JC12 @G@@@[          DS        A1,MULT(1,1).  STORE IN D1. WY
)@@G@@                   JC12 @G@@@[ DO SE ,  J         MULT(1,5).     SUCCESSWZ
)@@G@@ EXIT.                   JC12 @G@@@[.                                   XA
)@@G@@                               JC12 @G@@@[FAIL      LOCC      MULT(1,4),XB
)@@G@@$.   DEFINE FAILURE EXIT.            JC12 @G@@@[          END.      MULTXC
)@@G@@.                                          JC12 @I@@@@. ****************XD
)@@G@@*****************************************MULT****JC00             @I@@@@XE
)@@G@@. *********************************************************MULTC***JC00 XF
)@@G@@            @I@@@@MULTC**   PROC      1,4.               MULTIPLY ADDRESXG
)@@G@@S BY CONSTANT                 @I@@@@BITS*     FUNC.                     XH
)@@G@@   FIND OUT IF NUMBER IS A POWER OF 2           @I@@@@N         EQU     XI
)@@G@@  BITS(1).                                                        @I@@@@XJ
)@@G@@J  DO 35 , DO N--1*/J=0 , END J.                                        XK
)@@G@@            @I@@@@          END       0.                                XL
)@@G@@                              @I@@@@N         EQU       MULTC(1,3).     XM
)@@G@@                                                @I@@@@S         EQU     XN
)@@G@@  BITS(N).                                                        @I@@@@XO
)@@G@@ML        EQU       S=0.                                                XP
)@@G@@            @I@@@@          LA        A0,MULTC(1,2).                    XQ
)@@G@@                              @I@@@@  DO ML , MSI,U     A0,N.           XR
)@@G@@                                                @I@@@@  DO 1-ML , LSSL  XS
)@@G@@  A0,S.                                                           @I@@@@XT
)@@G@@          SA        A0,MULTC(1,1).                                      XU
)@@G@@            @I@@@@          SZ        MULTC(1,1)+1.                     XV
)@@G@@                              @I@@@@          END.                      XW
)@@G@@                                                @I@@@@. ****************XX
)@@G@@*****************************************MULTC***JC00             @I@@@@XY

)@@G@@*****PLUGTB**JC00             @I@@@@. PLUGTB  TABLE,KEY,SPEC.          'YV
)@@G@@PLUG SYNTAX TABLE'             JC30             @I@@@@.                 YW
)@@G@@                                                 JC30             @I@@@@YX
)@@G@@. KEY IS A VALUE TO BE PUT IN AS A TAG FOR THE ENTRIES IN THE SYNTAJC30 YY
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. TABLE 'TABLE' THAT CORRESPOND TO THE CHARACTERS IN TYZ
)@@G@@HE STRING    JC30             @I@@@@. POINTED TO BY SPEC.  IF KEY = CONTZA
)@@G@@IN, A TAG OF 0 IS ASSUMED, AND JC30             @I@@@@. ADDRESS PART IS ZB
)@@G@@FILLED OUT WITH THE OFFSET FOR TABLE.            JC30             @I@@@@ZC
)@@G@@.                                                                  JC30 ZD
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. X1, X4, A0-A5 USED.                                 ZE
)@@G@@             JC30             @I@@@@.                                   ZF
)@@G@@                               JC30             @I@@@@PLUGTB**  PROC    ZG
)@@G@@  1.                                             JC30             @I@@@@ZH
)@@G@@          LA,U      A1,PLUGTB(1,2).     TAG.                       JC30 ZI
)@@G@@            @I@@@@          LA        A2,PLUGTB(1,3).     A(SPEC).      ZJ
)@@G@@             JC30             @I@@@@          AA,H2     A2,PLUGTB(1,3)+2ZK
)@@G@@.   ADD OW(SPEC) = LOC OF STRINJC30             @I@@@@          LA,H1   ZL
)@@G@@  A3,PLUGTB(1,3)+2.   OC(SPEC) = CHAR WITHIN WORDJC30             @I@@@@ZM
)@@G@@          LA        A5,PLUGTB(1,3)+3.   L(SPEC) = NUMBER OF CHARS  JC30 ZN
)@@G@@            @I@@@@          LXI,U     A2,1.                             ZO
)@@G@@             JC30             @I@@@@          LXI,U     A3,1.           ZP
)@@G@@                               JC30             @I@@@@          JNZ     ZQ
)@@G@@  A1,PLUGYY.          IS KEY = CONTIN?           JC30             @I@@@@ZR
)@@G@@          LA,U      A1,PLUGTB(1,1).     IF SO, USE TABLE OFFSET    JC30 ZS
)@@G@@            @I@@@@          ANA,U     A1,TABLES.                        ZT
)@@G@@             JC30             @I@@@@          J         PLUGYY.         ZU
)@@G@@    GO GET A CHAR.             JC30             @I@@@@.                 ZV
)@@G@@                                                 JC30             @I@@@@ZW
)@@G@@PLUGXX    EX        CHRLX4,*A3.         X4 = CHAR OF STRING.       JC30 ZX
)@@G@@            @I@@@@          SA,H1     A1,PLUGTB(1,1),X4.  PUT VALUE IN HZY
)@@G@@1 OF ENTRY.  JC30             @I@@@@PLUGYY    JGD       A5,PLUGXX.      ZZ
)@@G@@    DECREMENT COUNT, REPEAT.   JC30             @I@]@@          LOFF.   AA
)@@G@@                                                 JC30             @I[@@@AB
)@@G@@          END.      PLUGTB.                                        JC30 AC
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. ****************************************************AD

)@@G@@PUTVC**   PROC      1,3.               PUT VALUE FIELD WITH OFFSET CONSTFH

)@@G@@                              @I@@@@          LA,H2     A1,PUTVC(1,3)+1.FJ
)@@G@@                                                @I@@@@          SA,H2   FK
)@@G@@  A1,1+PUTVC(1,2),A0.                                             @I@@@@FL
)@@G@@          END.                                                          FM

)@@G@@***********************RCALL***JC00             @I@@@@RCALL**   PROC    FP
)@@G@@  3.                 RECURSIVE CALL                               @I@@@@FQ
)@@G@@NARG      EQU       RCALL(2).                                           FR
)@@G@@            @I@@@@NOF2      EQU       (NARG=1)**RCALL(2,*1).            FS
)@@G@@                              @I@@@@NRET      EQU       RCALL(3).       FT
)@@G@@                                                @I@@@@P         EQU     FU
)@@G@@  RCALL(1,*1).                                                    @I@[@@FV
)@@G@@          LXI,U     CSTACK,2.                                           FW
)@@G@@            @I@[@@          SZ        A1.                               FX
)@@G@@                              @I@[@@          LA,U      A0,,OSTACK.     FY
)@@G@@                                                @I@[@@          LX,U    FZ
)@@G@@  OSTACK,,CSTACK.                                                 @I@[@@GA
)@@G@@          DS        A0,2,*CSTACK.                                       GB
)@@G@@            @I@[@@          LA,U      A0,LOC.                           GC
)@@G@@                              @I@[@@          DS        A0,2,*CSTACK.   GD
)@@G@@                                                @G@@@[          LXI,U   GE
)@@G@@  CSTACK,2.      STATE INFO FOR RETURN:          JC05 @G@]@[          LAGF
)@@G@@        A0,OSTACK.     A-FIELD = OLD STACK POINTER     JC05 @G@]@[      GG
)@@G@@    LA,U      A1,LOC.        V-FIELD = RETURN ADDRESS        JC05 @G@]@[GH
)@@G@@          LX        OSTACK,CSTACK. CURRENT TOP BECOMES 'OLD' TOP   JC05 GI
)@@G@@@G@]@[          DS        A0,2,*CSTACK.  STACK STATE INFO.              GJ
)@@G@@ JC05 @G@@[]          LA,U      A1,0.          FV-FIELDS SET TO ZERO;   GK
)@@G@@       JC05 @G@@[]          LA        A0,OSTACK.     OLD STACK POINTER. GL
)@@G@@             JC05 @G@@[]          LX        OSTACK,CSTACK. SAVE CSTACK IGM
)@@G@@N OSTACK.          JC05 @G@@[]          DS        A0,2,*CSTACK.  STACK PGN
)@@G@@REVIOUS OSTACK.          JC05 @G@@[]          LA,U      A0,LOC.        RGO
)@@G@@ETURN LOCATION.                JC05 @G@@[]          DS        A0,2,*CSTAGP
)@@G@@CK.  STACK IT, TOO.                  JC05 @I^@@@  DO 1-NOF2 ,J DO NARG ,GQ
)@@G@@  PUSH2  RCALL(2,NARG+1-J).                                 @I@@@@      GR
)@@G@@    J         RCALL(1,2).                                               GS
)@@G@@      @I@@@@  DO P ,LOC NOP     0.                                      GT
)@@G@@                        @I@@@@  DO 1-P ,LOC DS    A0,RCALL(1,1).        GU
)@@G@@                                          @I@@@@LOCND     EQU       $+NRGV
)@@G@@ET.                                                         @I@@@@J    DGW
)@@G@@O NRET ,L(J)  LOCC  RCALL(3,J),LOCND.                        JC02       GX
)@@G@@      @I@@@@J DO NRET , J       L(J).                                   GY
)@@G@@                        @I@@@@          END.                            GZ
)@@G@@                                          @I@@@@. **********************HA
)@@G@@***********************************RCALL***JC00             @I@@@@. ****HB
)@@G@@*****************************************************RCOMP***JC30       HC
)@@G@@      @I@@@@. RCOMP  D1,D2,GT,EQ,LT.           'REAL COMPARISON'        HD
)@@G@@       JC30             @I@@@@.                                         HE
)@@G@@                         JC30             @I@@@@. IF A(D1) > A(D2) THEN HF
)@@G@@GO TO GT;                                  JC30             @I@@@@. IF AHG
)@@G@@(D1) = A(D2) THEN GO TO EQ;                                  JC30       HH
)@@G@@      @I@@@@. IF A(D1) < A(D2) THEN GO TO LT;                           HI
)@@G@@       JC30             @I@@@@.                                         HJ
)@@G@@                         JC30             @I@@@@. A(D1) AND A(D2) ARE REHK
)@@G@@AL NUMBERS.                                JC30             @I@[@@. SEE HL
)@@G@@ACOMP FOR FURTHER INTO.                                      JC30       HM
)@@G@@      @G@@@[. SEE ACOMP FOR FURTHER INFO.                               HN
)@@G@@       JC00 @I@@@@.                                                     HO

)@@G@@            @I@@@@.                                                     HY

)@@G@@N CASE OF FAULT.               JC12 @I@@@@          LA        A0,RCOMP(1IA
)@@G@@,1). A(D1).                          JC30             @I@@@@          FAIB

)@@G@@,5). LT TEST.                        JC30             @I@@@@.           IG

)@@G@@ELFST**JC15*@G@@@[. RELFST  DE.                      'RELEASE FREE STORANK
)@@G@@GE'          JC15 @G@@@[.                                               NL
)@@G@@                   JC15 @G@@@[. DECREASE THE SIZE OF FREE STORAGE BY (ATNM
)@@G@@ MOST) A(DE) WORDS.      JC15 @G@@@[. A(TLSGP1) IS ONE GREATER THAN THE NN
)@@G@@LAST AVAILABLE ADDRESS; IT     JC15 @G@@@[. SHOULD BE ADJUSTED TO POINT NO
)@@G@@TO ONE PAST THE NEW TOP OF FREE      JC15 @G@@@[. STORAGE.  IF NOT IMPLENP
)@@G@@MENTED, RELFST SHOULD DO NOTHING AT ALL.   JC15 @G@@@[.                 NQ
)@@G@@                                                 JC15 @G@@@[. A0 USED.  NR
)@@G@@                                                       JC15 @G@@@[.     NS
)@@G@@                                                             JC15 @G@@@[NT
)@@G@@RELFST**  PROC      1.                                             JC15 NU
)@@G@@@G@@@[. THE LCORE$ EXECUTIVE REQUEST DOESN'T CURRENTLY WORK ON THE 1108.NV
)@@G@@ JC15 @G@@@[. THE CODE TO USE IT HAS BEEN WRITTEN AND SOMEWHAT CHECKED ONW
)@@G@@UT (AS JC15 @G@@@[. MUCH AS COULD BE DONE WITHOUT ACTUALLY HAVING THE FANX
)@@G@@CILITY), AND JC15 @G@@@[. WHEN LCORE$ BECOMES AVAILABLE, SNOBOL4 CAN BE NY
)@@G@@MADE TO USE IT BY  JC15 @G@@@[. ENABLING THE FOLLOWING MACRO DEFINITION:NZ
)@@G@@                         JC15 @G@@@[.                                   OA
)@@G@@                               JC15 @G@@@[.         LA        A0,TLSGP1.OB
)@@G@@     GET CURRENT TOP + 1.            JC15 @G@@@[.         ANA       A0,ROC
)@@G@@ELFST(1,1). CHOP OFF AMOUNT TO RELEASE     JC15 @G@@@[.         ANA,U   OD
)@@G@@  A0,1.          - 1, BECAUSE OF THE '+1'.       JC15 @G@@@[.         EROE
)@@G@@        LCORE$.        RELEASE IT.                     JC15 @G@@@[.     OF
)@@G@@    AND,U     A0,0777.       ADJUST TO NEXT MULTIPLE OF 512: JC15 @G@@@[OG
)@@G@@.         ANA       A0,A1.                                         JC15 OH
)@@G@@@G@@@[.         AA,U      A0,01001.      A0 = 1 + LAST VALID ADDRESS.   OI
)@@G@@ JC15 @G@@@[.         SA        A0,TLSGP1.     PUT IT IN A(TLSGP1).     OJ
)@@G@@       JC15 @G@@@[          END.      RELFST.                           OK
)@@G@@             JC15 @G@@@[. **********************************************OL

)@@G@@LINT***JC30             @I@@@@. RLINT  D1,D2,FAIL,SUCC.          'CONVERPV
)@@G@@T REAL TO INTEGER'       JC30             @I@@@@.                       PW
)@@G@@                                           JC30             @I@@@@. SETSPX
)@@G@@ A(D1) TO THE INTEGRAL PART OF A(D2), A REAL NUMBER.         JC30       PY

)@@G@@4 USED.                                                      JC30       QD

)@@G@@       JC30             @I@@@@RLINT**   PROC      1.                    QF
)@@G@@                         JC30             @I@@@@          LUF       A0,RQG
)@@G@@LINT(1,2). A0 = BIASED EXPONENT, A1 = MANTIJC30             @I@@@@      QH
)@@G@@    ANA,U     A0,0200.       A0 = ACTUAL EXPONENT.           JC30       QI
)@@G@@      @I@@@@          JN        A0,TOOSMALL.   IF A0 <= 0, RESULT IS < 1QJ
)@@G@@.      JC30             @I@[@@          TLE,U     A0,35.         IF > 35QK
)@@G@@, TOO BIG TO BE AN INTEGEJC30             @I@@@@          TG,U      A0,3QL
)@@G@@6.         IF A0 GT 35, TOO BIG TO BE INTEGJC30             @I@@@@      QM
)@@G@@    J         FAIL.                                          JC30       QN
)@@G@@      @I@@@@          DSA       A1,27.         A1 = 0 IF POS, -0 IF NEG.QO
)@@G@@       JC30             @I@@@@.                                  A2 = MAQP
)@@G@@NTISSA, LEFT-JUSTIFIED.  JC30             @I@@@@          LDSL      A1,0QQ
)@@G@@,A0.       SHIFT A1,2 LEFT A0 BITS TO PUT  JC30             @I@@@@.     QR
)@@G@@                             INTEGRAL PART IN A1.            JC30       QS
)@@G@@      @I@@@@GOTIT.                             GOT RESULT IN A1.        QT
)@@G@@       JC30             @I@@@@          SA        A1,RLINT(1,1). A(D1) :QU
)@@G@@= RESULT.                JC30             @I@@@@          LA,U      A1,IQV
)@@G@@NTDT.      FV(D1) := 0, INTEGER TYPE.      JC30             @I@@@@      QW
)@@G@@    SA        A1,RLINT(1,1)+1.                               JC30       QX
)@@G@@      @I@@@@          J         SUCC.          SUCCESS.                 QY
)@@G@@       JC30             @I@@@@.                                         QZ
)@@G@@                         JC30             @I@@@@TOOSMALL  LA,U      A1,0RA
)@@G@@.          VALUE IS ZERO.                  JC30             @I@@@@      RB
)@@G@@    J         GOTIT.                                         JC30       RC
)@@G@@      @I@@@@.                                                           RD
)@@G@@       JC30             @I@@@@FAIL      LOCC      RLINT(1,3),$.  DEFINE RE
)@@G@@EXITS HERE.              JC30             @I@@@@SUCC      LOCC      RLINRF
)@@G@@T(1,4),$.                                  JC30             @I@]@@      RG
)@@G@@    LOFF.                                                    JC30       RH
)@@G@@      @I[@@@          END.      RLINT.                                  RI

)@@G@@***********************************************SNAP****JC10 @G@@[]. SNAPXR
)@@G@@  LOC,N,ID.                  'SNAPSHOT DUMP'                 JC10 @G@@[]XS
)@@G@@.                                                                  JC10 XT
)@@G@@@G@@[]. THIS PRINTS THE N WORDS STARTING AT LOC, IDENTIFIED BY THE      XU
)@@G@@ JC10 @G@@[]. STRING ID.  UNLIKE DUMPWDS, THE ARGUMENTS TO SNAP ARE     XV
)@@G@@       JC10 @G@@[]. THE ADDRESSES THEMSELVES AND NOT REGISTERS CONTAININXW
)@@G@@G THEM.      JC10 @G@@[].                                               XX
)@@G@@                   JC10 @G@@[]SNAP**    PROC      1.                    XY
)@@G@@                         JC10 @G@@[]LOC       EQU       SNAP(1,1).     LXZ
)@@G@@OCATION TO DUMP.               JC10 @G@@[]N         EQU       SNAP(1,2).YA
)@@G@@     NUMBER OF WORDS.                JC10 @G@@[]ID        EQU       SNAPYB
)@@G@@(1,3).     IDENTIFYING STRING.             JC10 @G@@[].                 YC
)@@G@@                                                 JC10 @G@@[]$(2),PKT  + YD
)@@G@@        ID.            PACKET FOR CALL OF SNAP$.       JC10 @G@@[]      YE
)@@G@@    +         N,LOC.                                         JC10 @G@@[]YF
)@@G@@          +         0.             FOR SAVING A0.                  JC10 YG
)@@G@@@G@@[].                                                                 YH
)@@G@@ JC10 @G@@[]$(1)      SA        A3,PKT+2.      SAVE A0.                 YI
)@@G@@       JC10 @G@@[]          LA,U      A0,PKT.        LOAD PACKET ADDRESSYJ
)@@G@@.            JC10 @G@@[]          ER        SNAP$.         DO THE DUMP. YK
)@@G@@                   JC10 @G@@[]          END.      SNAP.                 YL
)@@G@@                         JC10 @G@@[]. **********************************YM

)@@G@@E REGISTER R, DEPENDING ON WHAT SORT JC06             @I@]@@. REGISTER RCA
)@@G@@ IS.  THE RESULT WILL BE ONE OF:                       JC06             CB
)@@G@@@I@]@@.         SX        R,A,X,J+H.     IF R IS AN X-REGISTER.         CC

)@@G@@S THE STRING SP AS DESCRIBED BY D2, THE 'FILE CONTROL  JC00             DF

)@@G@@CTICAL.                              JC00             @I@@@@.           DT
)@@G@@                                                       JC00             DU

)@@G@@ JC00             @I@@@@. RESTRICTIONS IN THE FORTRAN I/O ROUTINES.     DW

)@@G@@. *********************************************************TESTF***JC07 LP
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. TESTF  DE,FL,FAIL,SUCC.     'TEST FLAG'             LQ
)@@G@@             JC07             @I@@@@.                                   LR
)@@G@@                               JC07             @I@@@@. F(DE) IF TESTED LS
)@@G@@TO SEE IF THE FLAG FL IS SET.  IF IT IS, TRANSFERJC07             @I@@@@LT
)@@G@@. IS TO SUCC; IF NOT, IT IS TO FAIL.  FL MUST BE A POWER OF 2 TO WOJC07 LU
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. CORRECTLY; ONLY THE LAST 16 BITS ARE SIGNIFICANT.  ILV
)@@G@@F FL=0, THE  JC07             @I@@@@. FAILURE EXIT WILL BE TAKEN, THOUGHLW
)@@G@@ THIS ISN'T REQUIRED BY THE    JC07             @I@@@@. DEFINITION OF THLX
)@@G@@E MACRO.                                         JC07             @I@@@@LY
)@@G@@.                                                                  JC07 LZ
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. A0 IS USED.                                         MA
)@@G@@             JC07             @I@@@@.                                   MB
)@@G@@                               JC07             @I@@@@TESTF**   PROC    MC
)@@G@@  1.                  (3-4 WORDS GENERATED.)     JC07             @I@@@@MD
)@@G@@FE        EQU       1-TESTF(1,*3).      FAILURE EXIT EXISTS.       JC07 ME
)@@G@@            @I@@@@SE        EQU       1-TESTF(1,*4).      SUCCESS EXIT EMF
)@@G@@XISTS.       JC07             @I@@@@.                                   MG
)@@G@@                               JC07             @I@@@@          LA,H1   MH
)@@G@@  A0,TESTF(1,1)+1.    F(DE).                     JC07             @I@@@@MI
)@@G@@ DO FE ,  TOP,U     A0,TESTF(1,2).      PARITY ODD IF FLAG EXISTS  JC07 MJ
)@@G@@            @I@@@@ DO 1-FE ,  TEP,U   A0,TESTF(1,2).      EVEN IF NOT.  MK
)@@G@@             JC07             @I@@@@ DO FE ,  J         TESTF(1,3).     ML
)@@G@@    FAIL EXIT, IF NEEDED       JC07             @I@@@@ DO SE ,  J       MM
)@@G@@  TESTF(1,4).    SUCCESS EXIT.                   JC07             @I@]@@MN
)@@G@@          LOFF.                                                    JC07 MO
)@@G@@            @I[@@@          END.                                        MP
)@@G@@             JC07             @I@@@@. **********************************MQ
)@@G@@***********************TESTF***JC07             @I@@@@. ****************MR
)@@G@@*****************************************TESTFI**JC07             @I@@@@MS
)@@G@@. TESTFI  DE,FL,FAIL,SUCC.         ' TEST FLAG INDIRECT'           JC07 MT
)@@G@@            @I@@@@.                                                     MU
)@@G@@             JC07             @I@@@@. THIS TESTS F(A(DE)) FOR THE FLAG FMV
)@@G@@L, AND BRANCHES TO SUCC IF IT  JC07             @I@@@@. IS FOUND, AND TOMW
)@@G@@ FAIL IF NOT.  LIKE FOR TESTF, FL MUST BE A POWERJC07             @I@@@@MX
)@@G@@. OF 2, AND ONLY THE LAST 16 BITS ARE SIGNIFICANT.                 JC07 MY
)@@G@@            @I@@@@.                                                     MZ
)@@G@@             JC07             @I@@@@. A0 USED.                          NA

)@@G@@             JC07             @I@]@@          LOFF.                     NP

)@@G@@*****TOP*****JC03             @I@@@@. TOPBLK  D1,D2,D3.                'NZ

)@@G@@                                                 JC00             @I@@@@OB
)@@G@@. THIS SCANS BACKWARDS FOR THE 'TOP' OF A BLOCK OF MEMORY.  ITS    JC00 OC
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. NAME IS DIFFERENT FROM THE STANDARD SNOBOL4 MACRO DUOD
)@@G@@E TO CONFLICTJC00             @I@@@@. WITH THE 1108 'TOP' COMMAND (WHICHOE
)@@G@@ IS USED BY THIS MACRO).       JC00             @I@@@@. A BLOCK STARTS WOF
)@@G@@ITH A DESCRIPTOR WITH THE TTL FLAG SET.  A(D3)   JC00             @I@@@@OG
)@@G@@. GIVES THE ADDRESS OF THE LAST WORD OF THE BLOCK; SCANNING STARTS JC00 OH
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. WITH THIS DESCR (WHICH MAY BE A TTL) AND EACH PRECEDOI
)@@G@@ING DESCR    JC00             @I@@@@. IS EXAMINED UNTIL A TTL FLAG IS FOOJ
)@@G@@UND.  A(D1) IS THEN SET TO THE JC00             @I@@@@. ADDRESS OF THE SOK
)@@G@@TART OF THE BLOCK, AND A(D2) IS SET TO A(D3)-A(D1JC00             @I@@@@OL
)@@G@@. THE SIZE IN WORDS OF THE BLOCK.  FV(D1) IS SET TO FV(D3); FV(D2) JC00 OM
)@@G@@            @I@@@@. IS SET TO 0.                                        ON

)@@G@@***********************************INVOKE**JC21 @G@@@@.      RCALL  X,INZG
)@@G@@VOKE Y FAIL,NRET,VRET.                           JC21 @G@@@@.           ZH
)@@G@@                                                       JC21 @G@@@@. THISZI
)@@G@@ INVOKES THE INTERPRETER FUNCTION DESCRIBED BY Y AS FOLLOWS: JC21 @G@@@@ZJ
)@@G@@.      A(Y) = THE FUNCTION, A LOCATION IN FTABLE.                  JC21 ZK
)@@G@@@G@@@@.      V(Y) = THE NUMBER OF PARAMETERS IN THE CODE STREAM.        ZL
)@@G@@ JC21 @G@@@@.      F(Y) HAS THE 'FNC' FLAG SET.                         ZM
)@@G@@       JC21 @G@@@@. THE VALUE RETURNED WILL BE ASSIGNED TO X.  IF THE VAZN
)@@G@@LUE IS NAMED,JC21 @G@@@@. X WILL POINT TO ITS NAME AND EXIT 2 (NRET) WILZO
)@@G@@L BE TAKEN; IF THE JC21 @G@@@@. VALUE IS UNNAMED, X WILL POINT TO THE VAZP
)@@G@@LUE ITSELF AND EXIT 3    JC21 @G@@@@. (VRET) WILL BE TAKEN.  FAILURE (EXZQ
)@@G@@IT 1) WILL NORMALLY CAUSE      JC21 @G@@@@. A VALUE OF 0/0/0 TO BE RETURZR
)@@G@@NED, BUT THIS MAY NOT ALWAYS BE TRUE.JC21 @G@@@@.                       ZS
)@@G@@                                           JC21 @G@@@@INVOKE PROK   *0. ZT

)@@G@@S.     JC21 @G@@@@       BRANIC INCL,*0.             JUMP TO THE FUNCTIOAA
)@@G@@N CODE.      JC21 @G@@@@. **********************************************AB

)@@G@@***********************************ARGS****JC21 @G@@@@.      RCALL  N,ARAD

)@@G@@                                                       JC21 @G@@@@. THISAF
)@@G@@ EVALUATES ALL THE REMAINING ARGUMENTS TO THE CURRENT        JC21 @G@@@@AG
)@@G@@. FUNCTION, AND PUTS THEM ON THE STACK.  THE NUMBER OF ARGUMENTS   JC21 AH
)@@G@@@G@@@@. TO EVALUATE MUST BE IN A(PARAMS), AND THIS NUMBER WILL BE THE   AI
)@@G@@ JC21 @G@@@@. VALUE RETURNED IF ARGS SUCCEEDS.  NOTE:  IF ANY ARGUMENT FAJ
)@@G@@AILS,  JC21 @G@@@@. THE FAILURE EXIT WILL IMMEDIATELY BE TAKEN, AND THE AK
)@@G@@REST OF THE  JC21 @G@@@@. ARGUMENTS WILL REMAIN UNEVALUATED.  THE VALUE AL
)@@G@@RETURNED IN THIS   JC21 @G@@@@. CASE IS RATHER UNPREDICTABLE, AS IS THE AM

)@@G@@                               JC21 @G@@@@.                             AO

)@@G@@AL PARAMETERS LEFT IN    JC21 @G@@@@. THE CODE STREAM.  IF A(N) > A(PARADV
)@@G@@MS), NULL STRINGS WILL BE      JC21 @G@@@@. STACKED TO MAKE UP THE DIFFEDW
)@@G@@RENCE; IF A(N) < A(PARAMS), NOT ALL  JC21 @G@@@@. OF THE ARGS WILL BE EVDX
)@@G@@ALUATED, AND A(PARAMS) WILL BE THE NUMBER  JC21 @G@@@@. LEFT OVER.  NOTEDY
)@@G@@ THAT, UNLIKE 'ARGS', 'NARGS' DOESN'T RETURN A   JC21 @G@@@@. VALUE--THEDZ
)@@G@@ CALLING CODE MUST REMEMBER HOW MANY ARGS IT ASKED FOR.JC21 @G@@@@. IN EEA
